<p><b>Paramount Pictures Corporation</b> (also known as <b>Paramount Pictures</b> and simply <b>Paramount</b>) is an American <a href="/wiki/Film_studio" title="Film studio">film studio</a> based in <a href="/wiki/Hollywood" title="Hollywood">Hollywood</a>, <a href="/wiki/California" title="California">California</a>, that has been a subsidiary of the American <a href="/wiki/Media_conglomerate" title="Media conglomerate">media conglomerate</a> <a href="/wiki/Viacom" title="Viacom">Viacom</a>. Paramount is the fifth oldest surviving film studio in the world,<sup id="cite_ref-Abel10_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Abel10-2">[2]</a></sup> the second oldest in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>, and the sole member of the <a href="/wiki/Major_film_studio" title="Major film studio">"Big Six" film studios</a> still located in the <a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles" title="Los Angeles">Los Angeles</a> neighborhood of Hollywood. In 1916, film producer <a href="/wiki/Adolph_Zukor" title="Adolph Zukor">Adolph Zukor</a> contracted 22 actors and actresses and honored each with a star on the logo. These fortunate few would become the first "movie stars."<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup> Paramount Pictures is a member of the <a href="/wiki/Motion_Picture_Association_of_America" title="Motion Picture Association of America">Motion Picture Association of America</a> (MPAA).<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup></p>
<p>In 2014, Paramount Pictures became the first major Hollywood studio to distribute all of its films in digital form only.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup></p>
<p></p>
